    // Mega 5, 6, 7 y 8 DESKTOP
				function setLazyFrom(selector, firstLazyPosition) {
					document.querySelectorAll(selector).forEach(function (element, index) {
					   var position = (index + 1);
					   if (position >= firstLazyPosition) {
					      element.setAttribute('data-ad-lazy', 'true');
					   }
					});
				}
				
				setLazyFrom('[data-ad-type=mega][data-ad-device=md]', 2);
				// Mega 2, 3, 4, 5, 6, 7 y 8 MOBILE
				setLazyFrom('[data-ad-type=mega][data-ad-device=xs]', 2);
				// Roba 7 y 8
				setLazyFrom('[data-ad-type=roba][data-ad-device=md]', 4);
				setLazyFrom('[data-ad-type=roba][data-ad-device=xs]', 4);
				
				//Modulo 1
				setLazyFrom('[data-ad-type=modulo][data-ad-device=xs]', 1);
				
				//Cintillo 1 MOBILE
				setLazyFrom('[data-ad-type=cintillo-bn][data-ad-device=xs]', 1);

				
				// Roba 3 y 4 DESKTOP
				function setLazy(selector, lazyPosition) {
					document.querySelectorAll(selector).forEach(function (element, index) {
					   var position = (index + 1);
					   element.setAttribute('data-ad-type', 'roba' + position);
					   if (position == lazyPosition) {
					      element.setAttribute('data-ad-lazy', 'true');
					   }
					});
				}
				// Roba 3 y 4 DESKTOP
				setLazy('[data-ad-type=roba][data-ad-device=md]', 3);
				setLazy('[data-ad-type=roba][data-ad-device=md]', 4);

				
				// Roba 4 MOBILE
				setLazy('[data-ad-type=roba][data-ad-device=xs]', 4);
			
				
			godo.ads.push(function(x) {x.display("[data-ad-lazy=false]")});
   </script>
